Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	 One who is affected by swelling of the vein is recognized by its disposition upon being touched with fingers, and one can easily make an incision on this similarity, and on other parts of the body; and it is done by cutting the corner of the kidneys, then stretching the egg upwards, and drawing out the white sifac, and freeing the suspensory from all sides of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	 If the egg is already hardened with these new growths, then one must remove the egg and cut it; and if it is adhered to the sifac, or within what is in the vessels, then one must free all of this tension, and cut it evenly.[Original request fulfilled]
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	 And if the birth of the flesh is in the place behind, you should cut it all away and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when your work is completed, apply the wound with wet wool in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	 of the abscess of the haunches (buttocks)
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	 This is an abscess enclosed in a swelling resembling a hump, with softening of the haunches (buttocks), and the patient moves with difficulty when they walk; and the treatment for this illness is as fearsome as the one mentioned before, but nonetheless we will tell you the work of it, according to what the ancients did.[Answer: ] This is a description of an abscess located in the buttocks region. It is covered by a swelling that resembles a hump, and the surrounding area is soft or weakened. The patient experiences difficulty when walking. The treatment for this condition is said to be as fearsome as the previous one mentioned, but the text will still describe the procedure based on what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	 It is necessary that you make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then place the suspension of the loins below your hands, on all the vessels that are close to the groin, and tie it tightly; and stretch it widely; then cut with a sharp knife in a straight line across the vessels, until they are exposed; and then flay from both sides, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries which are in the temples; then insert a needle where there is a double thread, and bind it to the first place where the vein has come, and bind it again to the other end; then cut straight in the middle, according to the length of the body, and remove the corrupted moisture; then cure the wound as the others who are injured, so that any vessel which is cut may be nourished by one of the groins; for by this no harm comes, and if veins from all sides come, then the groins must be bound to all the vessels; so that the eye does not lose its nourishment because of the incision of the vessels, and they dry out and cannot help each other.
de la routure dou syfac	 of the rupture of the syphilis sore
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	 The events of this rhizome (ramice) come about from the rupture that occurs in the syphilis sore or the extension on the belly in the region of the haunches, causing the intestines to descend from the rupture to one of the hips; and this rupture is either in the syphilis sore or in the extension of it, and these two manners come about from many causes: from percussion, jumping, coughing, lifting heavy objects, and similar things; and the signs when it is due to the extension of the syphilis are that it occurs frequently over a long period and does not happen suddenly; and the abscess is even on the surface down to its depth because the syphilis attracts the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	 And the sign is when it is of the rupture of the syphilitic sore, that it brings about sudden pain at the beginning, and is the diverse appearing abscesses under the skin close by, and this is due to the evacuation of the intestine and flesh from the defect of the syphilitic sore.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	 And sometimes the guts slip out with the intestines, and are retained inside, causing great pain to the patient, even when pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	 And in these cures involving iron, there is reason to be afraid, so it is necessary to withdraw from it.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	 And the method of this treatment is as follows: you instruct the patient to pull the intestines back into the wound with their hand if they can; then support their neck between your hands and raise their hips; then extend their kidneys upward, and cut all the skin from the genitals along the long side; then insert the books of the loin with hooks according to what you need to open the wound, making sure the intestines can exit; then skin the syphilitic sore that is under the genital skin until the white syphilitic sore is exposed on all sides; then insert your index finger into the part that follows the genitals, between the white syphilitic sore and the second syphilitic sore, and separate it from what is behind the loin and the second syphilitic sore; and move your right hand inside the kidneys, extending the white syphilitic sore up to your left hand, and lift the loin toward the flank of the wound; and instruct the assistant to stretch the loin upward and untie what is behind it; and check with your fingers if any part of the intestines is wrapped in the white syphilitic sore, and if you find anything, place it back inside the abdomen; then take a needle with thick thread made of ten strands, and insert it into the back part of the syphilitic sore, which is after the genital skin; then cut the edges that appear from the threads until there are four strands left; then arrange them like a cross and bind the syphilitic sore, which is under the genital skin, with a strong ligature of two parts; then wrap the thread edges and bind them firmly with two parts, so that no blood can enter and cause an abscess; and place another ligature according to the first long ligament, leaving a space of two fingers from the syphilitic sore that is under the kidneys; and after these two ligatures, leave the syphilitic sore exposed for the width of one finger; and finally, cut the part that is under the genital skin until the fat comes out, and the bowel is exposed, as we have said before; then apply wet wool to the wound and place the ligature that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	 And sometimes the white pus-filled abscesses that we mentioned are cauterized after incision, due to fear of spread of blood.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 For this often happens, and leave the abscess intact until it bursts on its own; and if it does not break open quickly, apply hot water and use what we mentioned earlier, until it bursts; then cure the wound with other treatments, until it is healed perfectly.
de hernie carnouse	 of a fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	 In this type, I have never seen anyone who dared to perform the cure with iron.[translated by user:chatGPT]
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And the ancients said that it is formed in the same way as the ramus (?) that is attached to the spine, in such a manner that you bind the vessels after making an incision lightly above it; then cut in between and cure the abscess with what one does, until the vessels burst; and cure it as we have said, until it is healed.[translated by user:chatGPT]
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres; et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent; et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert; et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois; et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre; puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines; puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	 Sometimes there comes a rupture in the entrails, as we have said, and the place is visible; and none of the intestines come out at the opening, and if any do come out, it is little, and it goes back in within the hour; and nevertheless, if it stays in this state for too long, the wound or abscess grows larger until the intestine comes out; and this happens due to the swelling of the abscess in the entrails, as we have said, for it becomes swollen and inflamed, making the place visible and open; and the cure is by cauterization, as we have previously mentioned; and sometimes it is cured by iron in this manner: and it is that the patient lies on their back between your hands, then cut the swollen part of the rupture to the width of three fingers; and then remove the abscess which is beneath the skin that has grown over it, then take the fat and place it on the visible surface of the abscess; and press it deep into the belly, then cut the two visible parts of the abscess on the end of the fat, cutting one and the other; then remove the end of the fat, and do not cut or stretch the abscess or anything else, as I have made you know in the cure of the ramicum of the intestines; then cure it by the cure of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And when you cut the veins, clean and care for the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	 The syphilitic patient is constricted, and shows no sign of improvement, and the cautery is more appropriate in this case, and closer to a cure.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	 of the softening of the skin of the buttocks
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	 The skin of the buttocks is often softened in some men due to the internal organs being weakened and it is visible; and if one wants to treat it, make the patient lie on their stomach, then cut the softened skin that is above the natural skin; then bring the two sides together with a stitch, and if you see excess softened skin, remove it with three or four firm stitches; then cut between the stitches and treat it like other wounds until it heals, and let the sutures fall out.
dou chastrement	 of the castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	 Know that surgery is prohibited in our religion, and for this reason, I would not like to speak of it in this book; and it is necessary for two reasons: one is so that the physician can give knowledgeable responses when asked about it and know how to cure; and the other is because we often need to perform surgery on certain animals to help us, such as castration of a goat, sheep, pig, and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	 I therefore say that surgery is performed in two ways: either by pulling or by cutting open.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	 In the one done by pulling, we make the animal sit in hot water until the joints become soft and pliable, then grab hold of them with your hand and pull until they are back in place and you no longer feel resistance.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 Of the castration procedure: you must stain the animal, and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut each testicle with one stroke, after they have been well flayed; and leave some tissue of the epididymis and the delicate epididymis which is above the vessels; and this method of castration is safer than that made by attraction, because in attraction there may remain something of the testicles, for which reason the animal still desires lust; then cure the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	 Of hermaphrodites: when a person is born with both male and female genitalia, it is necessary to examine the situation carefully. If there is a predominance of male characteristics, the person should be considered male. If there is a predominance of female characteristics, the person should be considered female. In cases where the genitalia are equally developed or ambiguous, the decision as to which gender the person should identify as should be based on other factors such as the person's internal sense of self and their personal identification with one gender over the other. It is important to note that in medieval medicine, intersex individuals were often seen as "monstrous" or "abnormal", but modern medical understanding recognizes that they are simply a natural variation in human development. The key point is to treat all individuals with respect and dignity, regardless of their physical characteristics or gender identity.
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	 Hermaphrodite is of two kinds in men: one kind is that between the two thighs it opens as wide as the shape of a woman's nature, with hair present, and sometimes urine flows from it.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	 And the other kind is in women, with a protrusion like a penis and two thighs.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	 And the treatment for both, male and female, is to cut away the adjoined flesh and treat it like other wounds. In the second case, of males who urinate through the skin of the thighs, there is no cure.

Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	 Tumor is a growth attached to the nail, so long that it is unsightly; and some women have them as large as a hand, and this is its cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	 It is necessary to dye the excess of the tumor with your hand or with tweezers, and pluck it gently; and do not go too deep, so that bleeding does not occur, then cure another wound until it is healed; and at another growth that arises at the mouth of the sore, and apply it, and perhaps it will come out, and it resembles a cow's udder, and for this reason, the ancients called it "cow disease.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 It is necessary to pluck it, as we have said, the tumor, and cure it until it is healed.
de erratique	 of erratics (dislocations)
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	 Erratics are when the nature of a woman is not perceived, or the opening is small; and it is natural at birth, or occurs by accident due to illness; or it is through artifice, such as a subtle or thin syphilitic chancre, and is located deep in the womb, on the sides, below, or elsewhere; and it prevents conception, childbirth, and possibly menstruation; and knowledge of this is gained through examination by a midwife.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	 If the stoppages are apparent and close, then use your fingers or a probe.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	 If it is a subtle syphilis and located two fingers away, then act quickly: place your two index fingers together, have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread apart; then fully extend the two fingers until they touch the subtle chancre and push past the obstruction; then take wool, soak it in oil, and place it on the area; have the woman lie with a man each day so that it does not heal shut.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	 And if the fig tree is hard and thick, it should be cut with a spatula resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If the stoppers are made of flesh, suspend them with a string and cut them; and have hemostatic medicines ready, such as acacia, dragon's blood, incense, plenty of egg; then prepare a wide wooden trough so that the wound cannot stick; and let it be like this for a long time, and apply a tent of dry linen to it; then let other wounds be treated until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	 And when flesh grows in the wound, it should be cut in this way, if it is not abscesses that have grown larger.[It's unclear what "marris" refers to without additional context. Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	 For a spreading abscess on the shin, one should not touch it with fire.
des emorroides	 of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	 Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that are not usually visible, and when hemorrhoids become old, they become thickened; and we have previously mentioned their likenesses, and signs, and I will say here those that receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	 I say that when hemorrhoids and thickened ones are inside the shin and not perceptible to touch, they cannot be cured by cauterization with fire.[References(s):](https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caut%C3%A8re)
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	 Those that are at the mouth of the shin, and can be felt, are those that can be cured.[References(s):](https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caut%C3%A8re)
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	 Then you should place the woman in a cool house, pull the tooth with pliers at the root, then apply powdered medicines that constrict blood, such as acacia and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things; then have her sit against the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water; and if bleeding occurs, make her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate bark and galls and similar things, and then take barley flour, mix it with honey and vinegar, and make a plaster to apply on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	 And if it stops (the bleeding), that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	 If not, apply cupping glasses to her back and breasts without causing injury; then take wool, soak it in plantain juice or hollyhock juice with old wine, and apply it to the affected area.[translatewiki:en]
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when the abscess rests, cure the area with a dressing until it is healed; and that which is called "albathir" is red, and looks like a rough surface, then it should be covered as I have said with a "thelul"; and then cure it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	 of abscesses in the wound/sore
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	 Many types of abscesses come to the wound/sore, such as chancre and abscess of pus, and herpes and carbuncles and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	 Therefore, I must speak in this treatise of the hot abscess that comes to the wound/sore, which is not one of those that collect pus; and if you wish to know the work of fire, see if the abscess is hard at the beginning of its appearance, full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	 Then do not rush to pierce, but let it subside until the pain is eased; and then have the patient sit on a seat, and have two small stools for them to lean back on, and support their back and bring their legs apart from the thighs; and let their thighs be spread out, and place their arms beneath their knees, and bind them well with a good ligament; then turn them towards the right side, and prepare the instrument that is used to treat the mouth of the wound, which will come later in the form; and it is necessary that when you intend to prepare this instrument, that you insert the style first to gauge the depth of the wound, so that what enters inside through the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and does not injure the patient; and if the instrument is larger, then cover the depth of the wound with rags, so that the instrument does not harm it; and it is necessary that they place the funnel of the instrument on top, and hold the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.	 And when the abscess opens, and it is cut open by hand, you should cover it with a wet lint; and once the boil is emptied, you should put damp bandages soaked in rose oil or dry vert oil into the wound; and push the bandage deep into the wound and place a clean, moist woolen cloth on top of the wound and on the bandage; then dress it for two days with appropriate ointment until it heals; and sometimes the wound and the abscess are raised with an enema of water and honey, and then with boiled water and lily roots and aristolochia longa; then return to the dressing.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	 And if the wound is inflamed, one should be careful not to apply a hot iron, but rather treat it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	 of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	 It is necessary for the midwife to first recognize the signs of a natural childbirth, and one such sign is when you see the woman pressing downwards and having the urge to smell things; then the child hastens to come out. So if you see these signs, you should gently press on her stomach so that the child comes out quickly. For when it descends onto its head, the afterbirth comes with it, and the womb is cleaned of its impurities by a good cleansing. And one who comes out differently does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	 For it happens sometimes that he comes to his feet, and the body or the head, and the hands, or it comes upon his belly, or often, and is turned by chance on his neck, and in other evil figures; so it is necessary for the balancer (i.e. the person in charge) to be wise and skillful in these things, and to be wary of error and deception, and I will show you all the figures (i.e. positions) how one should assist.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	 If the child comes out on his head by natural delivery, and the woman gives birth with difficulty, and her strength is weak, then make her sit on a saddle, or have women hold her; and apply oil or fenugreek that has been cooked to stimulate her labor, and then put the small spatula, of which this is the shape, between her thighs:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.	 and split the frenulum, and cut it to the nail so that the moisture which is inside comes out; and press the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to give an enema to the woman with a concoction of fenugreek and oil of St. John's wort; then make her drink a concoction and cause her to sneeze with spices, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour: the child will come out now.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	 And if both hands come out, you must gently and gradually put them back; and if they cannot enter, make the woman sit, and lift her feet up; then tilt the seat on the ground, and support the woman so that she does not fall during the procedure; and if the hands cannot enter, and the child is dead, cut the hands with the knife which is placed here in front, and extract the child, and also reset [the womb].
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	 of the child's coming-out (emergence) on its feet (standing)

de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	 of the birth of the child on its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc; puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit; et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval; et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains; et ewe l’enfant poc et poc; et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	 When the child comes in this form (i.e., breech position), place the woman's hands knees-to-knees; then support her neck, and let her legs hang down, and have her lie on the bed; fold her hands knees-to-knees, and then place your hands on her belly, and remove the small of her back; make sure she is prepared in this way; if the child does not come out on its own, take hold of its feet and pull firmly, then push on its belly, and introduce your hands; and deliver the child knees-first; and tell the woman to push when the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	 of the child's birth which comes out holding a hand askew.
I covient engignier a ramener la main: s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler; s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment; puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit; et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main; et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	 It is necessary to contrive a way to bring the hand back in: if it cannot be brought back, then make the woman stand up and walk; if she cannot walk, then make her lie down on a bed, and straighten out her legs strongly; then apply the method I have mentioned; and if she does not give birth, then make her sit on a seat, and then study how to bring the hand back in; and turn the child according to its natural shape, and make it sneeze, and command her to pull until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	 of the child's birth with its head up by its mother's neck, and its hands spread open, and its face turned towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement; et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc; et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	 It is necessary for the physician to take his hand, then turn it back and forth gently; and when it is even, place on it a small piece of raw meat and oil, as we have said; then instruct her to move it back and forth; and once you have done this, make her sit up and instruct her to take a deep breath; and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	 in the same manner for all the sutures.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie; et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes; puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois: adonques si istra legierement.	 When it comes to all the sutures in this manner, cut the suture at your nail, as much as necessary for the pus to drain; and if the child presses on its face and neck, cut from the mouth so that it is not retained, and the child will not die; then place the child back in, as much as needed, and instruct the woman to take a deep breath; and then it will come out easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	 of the dislocation of the calves (or lower leg)
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	 Know that calves are often born in pairs, and sometimes three or four at a time; and this is not a strange thing, it happens rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom; je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude; et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	 Two are strange things that do not live long, if they can be named; I know this, that they multiply and are separated by the syphac that divides them, which is attached to the belly; and sometimes they come out as naturally as lumps under the skin, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait; et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	 And if they come out roughly, treat them as we have said and let the surgeon be skillful, and do quickly and lightly what she does; and do it so that they are healed for good.[Notes: The word "griement" in Old French can mean roughly or painfully. The word "ceu" is a plural demonstrative pronoun that refers to the two strange things mentioned earlier, which I translated as "they". In this context, "li baile" (the surgeon) is feminine. Also, I used "healed for good" to translate "salut" because it can mean health or salvation in medical texts.]
de plusors enfans	 of several children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient; si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	 Certain times, formations occur in the marrow of the limb, either I, II, III, IV, V, VI, VII, or more up to XV, and they are all formed in the shape of a child according to the measurement of the wise physician. And it is necessary that the healer knows this, because by chance similar things happen; and do accordingly as is needed.
de l’enfant mort	 of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains; si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort; si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees; et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant; puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges; puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief; si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes; et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide; et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	 When you treat a woman for a stillborn child or swollen belly, as I have mentioned in the division, and it does not come out, and you are required to use your hands; then you must determine if the woman is of sound health, and if she has had no accident or is fearful of death; then the woman should be positioned on her back, with her hips tilted downward, and legs raised; and the attendant should dress her from two sides, so that she is tied to the bed so as not to hinder the descent of the child; then anoint the mouth of the widow with moist eyes with muscillage of althea and fenugreek and flaxseed, then anoint the nipples of her breasts with these oils and muscillages; then gently insert them into the widow, then watch carefully where she inserts the nipples so that they are suitable for this, and take care if the child is positioned head-down; then attach the nipple to her right hand, and place the basin between her hands of the left hand, and gently insert it with all her hand, and attach the nipple in one of the places we have mentioned, until it comes to the empty space; and this is the form of the nipple.
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz; et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	 then place against it another bandage, or a third if needed, so that the tractions are even; and then stretch it evenly by moving it back and forth, so that the dislocation is put back, and let the bandages be tightened to hold the dislocation in place, as follows:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie; et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	 And if any part of it remains, let the physician anoint some of his fingers with oil and insert them into that part, and pull the other part; and if there remains none, then place this bandage or higher up, and do so until everything comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote; puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	 And if one hand comes in front of the other and cannot be brought back by tightening, then you should wrap it in a cloth until it comes out completely; then bind it at the joint of the wrist or ankle, and do the same for the other hand and both feet.[`samarium`](https://stackoverflow.com/users/15064732/samarium)
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue; ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui; et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment; et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer; et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues; et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	 And if the child's head is large and tight in the opening, or if they have a swollen fontanelle, then you should insert the spatalium with spine between your fingers and make an incision in the fontanelle to drain the fluid; or you can puncture it with the instrument called "almidach," which is included in the set of instruments or chapter that comes after this one. And do the same if the infant has a naturally large head; then pull out the bones using tongs. If the head pops out and becomes constricted by the forceps, then split it open until the fluid in the fontanelle drains out. If it cannot drain on its own, then break it into pieces as much as you can; and if their belly or lower abdomen is bloated, then pierce it until the fluid runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	 And if the child is standing on its feet, the drawing up is light, and the leading to the mouth of the vein is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main; et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre; et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris; puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer; et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses; et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	 And if it is constricted in the belly or breast, you should draw it out with a cloth wrapped around your hand; and make an incision in the belly or breast, until the moisture that is there runs out; and if other limbs are removed and the head remains, you should put your finger deep into the vein and pull it to the mouth of the vein; then introduce one or two leeches and pull them out; and if the mouth of the vein is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has formed there, you should not work on it, but instead introduce moist and fatty substances; and apply soothing plasters and warm, softening and moistening compresses.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif; et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	 And if the infant is on its side and you can straighten it out, then moderate what we have said in the case of a living child; and if there is no power to do so, then pull it out in pieces, and leave nothing of the afterbirth behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris; et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	 And when you have done this, moderate what we have said in the case of abscesses that come in the womb; and if bleeding occurs, then apply cold compresses, and moderate other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	 And I saw a woman in whose womb one child had died, then another was sewn onto it, and the second one came to life.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	 After a long time, an abscess came in her belly, and it swelled so much that it burst open, and she began to suffer greatly.[Read more at StackExchange](https://french.stackexchange.com/questions/48215/translation-of-a-medical-text-from-the-13th-century)
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	 I was called to heal, and I thought for a long time, and the wound could not be healed.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	 I applied a strong plaster, and there came out a bone, and after several days, another one did.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	 I marveled greatly at this, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	 So I thought that it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point; et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu; et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	 I examined the wound and extracted many bones until the woman was in better condition; and she lived for a long time like this, with some fluid coming out of her side from time to time; and I have only recorded this chapter because when a master finds something strange, he should know how to provide help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	 to set the fracture back in its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	 Here comes the form of the tourniquet, with which to bind the books (?); and it has two turns around the two legs (?)
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux; et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi; et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus; et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	 Nonetheless, let the horns of the tourniquet be more slender than the restrictor, and let it be made of ebony or boxwood; and let the mouth of the staff be two fingers wide, and the margin of the branches one finger, and in length a palm and a half; and between the two limbs there should be two joints of this same wood, which are tightened in both, by half a palm long or a little more; and these two joints are placed in the mouth of the fracture to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles; et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large; et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes; puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	 Another form, of more subtle and lighter appearance, should be made from a ebony or boxwood stick, similar to the shape of pincers; and have at the two ends two grips, as you see, of one palm in length, and two fingers in width; and when you wish to open the wound with the entire instrument, make the woman sit on a bed, her legs spread apart and feet hanging down, then bring the two grips together in the wound, and hold the head of the instrument beneath her thighs; then work your hand with the entire instrument, just as you did with the pincers equally, according to the width that you wish to open the mouth of the wound, so much that the ball (of the instrument) does what it is supposed to.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	 These instruments are all long-handled, and they have many variations; and when the surgeons have prepared them, the work is quicker and higher for them due to their size.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	 Do not disdain the instrument because you have not prepared it, for their necessity is not to be excused.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis; et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	 When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the woman to hold her breath, and then make her sneeze with some substance, and hold her hands to her mouth and nose; and if she does so, it will be fine.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire; toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	 If not, take a pot, and make a hole in the cover, and put in herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as chamomile, rue, anise, camomile, casia, and centaury; all these herbs, or some of them, should be boiled in water over the fire; then place a reed or hole in the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the woman, and hold it there until the vapors enter the womb; then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	 If the sutures come out quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction; mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	 And if it remains after this treatment and does not come out, order the nurse to wet her left hand in oil of sesame or altea mucilage, and then insert it into the nature (vagina) and search for the suture; and when she has found it, take hold of it and pull it gently upwards and downwards, so that the knot does not tear during extraction; but it should be moved lightly to the right and left, and then pulled out; it will come out and dry up.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes; et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire; mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon; si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	 And if the mouth of the womb is too closed, we have said the cure is to induce sneezing and fumigation with herbs; and if it does not come out at all that we have mentioned, make sure not to force during extraction; but it is necessary for what is in the mouth of the womb to be tied to the thigh of the woman, then enema her with tetrapharmacum ointment; it will soften and bring it out, and it will come out; however, when it softens and comes out, there will be a bad smell in the stomach and head, and it will wound the patient.[translated by user-defined function]
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	 Then it is appropriate to use suitable fumigations for this: some of the ancients have tried fumigation of watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	 The shape of the instrument used to fumigate the woman for the retention of menses and secondary hemorrhage is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu; et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	 And it is made of glass, similar to a small chimney, with the narrow end placed in the nature (vagina), and the wide ends above the fire; the fumigation should be placed over the coals, and replaced when it has burned out, starting with a new one.
de percier lou fondement	 to pierce the anus
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac: si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche; puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Many children are born who do not have their anus pierced, but instead it is stopped with a thin membrane: then the midwife must carefully puncture this membrane with her instrument, and not with a sharp blade, making sure not to touch it; then place wet wool soaked in wine and oil over it, and keep applying the ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	 And if you doubt that it will stay (in place), put in a piece of wood made from elder tree, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the infant wants to go to rooms (chambers).
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	 And sometimes, these stoppages come from sudden wounds or abscesses; such a stoppage needs to be covered and treated, as we have said about the piece of wood made from elder tree.
de la fistule dou fondement	 of the fistula in the anus (bottom)
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	 Fistulas that come from under the anus are swelling and grow larger as they appear near the anus or in the space of two parts (of the body), having one or multiple fistulas; and when this swelling is old, it works (i.e., drains), and often produces whitish water or thin liquid, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent; and they are known by the fact that there is a discharge or gas when the patient makes defecation, and perhaps in his jump, a worm comes out.[Notes: "egestion" means excretion or elimination. "ventositeit" is probably a misspelling of "ventosité", which refers to flatulence or gas.]
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	 And if there are fistulas that reach to the bladder, and to the middle of the penis; and they reach to the joint of the thigh, and to the groin.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant: et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	 And so one recognizes the fistula reaching to the anus, and not reaching: and that is if you insert your index finger into the anus, and insert a thin needle of steel or iron into the fistula when there is no tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit; et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit: saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	 And if there is tortuosity, insert a thin probe of wood or horsehair until you feel it with your finger; and if you do not feel it, and it does not come out of the opening with egestion nor ventosities nor pus, as we have said: know that it does not penetrate; so hurry to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	 And when the fistula reaches down to the bladder or to the urethra's conduit, urine leaks out, and it cannot be healed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu; s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement; et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	 If it [the fistula] is pierced down to the joint of the thigh, then the vein extends down to that place; if there is no twisting and pain is not felt around it, then it is already bowed, and neither medicine nor a cure through ointment is effective; and in these pierced fistulas, there is no cure except labor and the folly of foolish practitioners who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre; puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	 In one that is not pierced and is not old, there is hope of healing through cauterization, as I have proven, and the patient should lie on their back in your hands; lift their legs up to their thighs, and have their thighs inclined towards their belly; then insert a tent of iron or of wood if there is twisting, until you know where the tent comes out.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans; si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	 If the patient feels it around the anus, you should insert your index finger, and if you feel that the abscess has burst; and have it uncovered where you feel, between your finger, the pus or flesh, then know that it is penetrated; do not work further on it, as it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc; et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit; et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil; et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	 Moreover, it is to be noted that some can indeed be cured, but this happens rarely; and the help that one can provide is to heat the cautery gently according to the width of the fistula, as has been said before; and insert it, very hot, into the fistula until it reaches near the anus; and do this two or three times, until you are certain that the decayed flesh, which resembles a bird's feather, is burnt; then cure it with moist bandages and butter, until the decayed flesh comes out; then cure it with a healing ointment that causes flesh to grow and heals.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	 If it is thus healed, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez; et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur; si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente; et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	 If it cannot be healed in any other way, and if it swells up and does not burst until it reaches the finger that is at its base, and there is a thick covering of flesh or membrane between your finger and the swelling, and you see the fistula following the covering of the skin; then cut from the beginning of the fistula, and push the swelling forward with your finger, and then use the cautery until you reach the tip of the swelling; and the swelling will be released and will fall off; then clean away the decayed flesh that looks like a bird's feather, and nothing will remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	 And if the blood flow overcomes you and flows between you and the procedure, then cauterize it with fire or a medicinal substance.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor; puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe; puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	 For the fire cautery brings about two good things: namely, the sear of the joined flesh, and the constriction of blood and the drying of moisture; then the treatment of swollen tents (boils) with butter or crushed herbs, until the place becomes suppurated and the burned flesh comes out in the pus; then heal the wound with dry medicinal substances that expel hardened pus.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	 For when it is healed, it is clean and will not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	 And if a fistula reaches down to the depth of the anus and is distant from the body, insert your finger into the anus and examine it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres: ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit; puis le cure, si com nos avons dit; par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé; puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues; puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	 If you feel the abscess, and between two are the cloth or syringe or probe, near to piercing, let there be nothing but a way of trust and hope, through the administration of one of the three methods: either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it down to the base, or if you can, place tents and cure it as before; and do not go too deep, so that you do not cut the support which holds the foundation, and waste products come out there without will; then cure, as we have said; perhaps it will be healed, or you remove that covering and clean it once it is cut next to the foundation, either with a tent or with another pointed instrument; then clean the cavity that is in the wound, as much as you can; then strive to restore the wound, and to maintain the fistula on the side outside the foundation: it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	 And sometimes fistulas occur in this manner: when you insert the probe into the fistula, and it is beside the base near the skin above, take a probe pierced at the tip in this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	 And insert an twisted wire into it (fistula), and insert the probe along the entire length of the wire in the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement; et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II; et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent; puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	 If it (fistula) is open at the edge of the base inside, then remove the wire from that hole, as if you were inserting your finger in the base; and pull the tip of the wire, and bring the two sides together, and hold them close to each other, and leave it for one or two days; and tighten it occasionally, until the wire cuts through those parts that are between (them), and become detached; then heal the wound until it is healed and cleaned up.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	 If the fistula does not pierce, make it pierce in all ways that you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 For one should not cover the wound so deeply with a bandage and then treat it, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans; et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	 The shape of the pointed spatula with which one forms the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting; and on the other side not, so that one does not cut what one should not cut, as you can see here:
des emorroydes	 of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors; et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz; si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines; et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot; et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere; ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez; et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement; cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere; et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	 Hemorrhoids are of two kinds: either they are inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and they often bleed, and there is one or more, and they are under the anus and at the anus; but those that are under it have little moisture, and still sometimes there is some watery humor or some blood, and they have the color of flesh; and the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you instruct the patient to strain when going to the bathroom, so that the anus protrudes and the threads appear; then hurry and pull it with pincers, or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its roots; and if the hooks cannot hold them due to their moisture, take a piece of fabric, cotton, or a piece of camelot and pull them out with your hands, then cut them, and sprinkle some hot powders on top that are in place of cauterization; or you can cauterize it as it is said in the chapter on cauterization, then treat them with other treatments until they are healed; and if the anus cannot come out, enema the patient with a bitter and harsh enema to clean what is in the anus, so that it may come out openly; when the patient feels ready, and when the threads have come out of the anus, then the treatment is easy; and it is that you take them with your nail or with pincers, and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and make the patient fear incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc; puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose; et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 You should prepare the suture in this manner: take a twisted thread and put it on a needle, then pull the thread over and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread beneath the needle, and let it be of sufficient length; pull the thread tight, then knot the thread, and remove the needle, and do the same with all the others, and leave one to correct any excess blood; then place a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or cerote on the wound, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest; and let it be so until they urinate, and when they have passed urine, cure it with ointment and other cures, until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	 dry pus or discharge
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	 Many times it happens that there is dry dung in the intestines, due to constipation of the body, and when the illness is old and medicine is not effective.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir; puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient; et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez; puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then you must scrape off the scab on top with the tip of a spatula or your nail, so as not to let it become wet; then cure it until it is solid as it should be; and if it cannot solidify, then repeat the shaving more vigorously than before, until it heals well and becomes scabbed; then cure it until it heals completely.
dou fremit	 trembling, shaking
